# Project State

## Project Reference

See: .paul/PROJECT.md (updated 2026-05-29)

**Core value:** Consolidates fragmented PSG tooling into one branded `hub.psgweb.me` surface that customers, internal staff, and superadmins all use — replacing logins and tooling sprawl with role-gated unified access.
**Current focus:** **⭐ Milestone v0.3 Customer Analytics 🚧 CREATED 2026-06-04 — 0 of 3 phases. Goal: fill the empty analytics surface with a unified Google Ads + GA4 + GSC + SEMrush marketing view, output as the automated PSG monthly client report (multi-LLM narrative + branded PDF). Phases: 9 Google Ads surface (BSM Phase 5 data, no OAuth; + MSO aggregate + switcher typeahead + LCP<2s gate) · 10 GA4+GSC+SEMrush unified (per-shop Google OAuth D68; SEMrush account-level MCP; refresh tokens pgsodium-encrypted) · 11 PSG report (narrative + PDF spec'd to the existing hand-built client deliverable, template canon = `archive/local_reach-outputs/`). Cut from v0.3 → v0.3.5+: presence/listings + post-repair sentiment. Next: `/paul:plan` Phase 9.** v0.2 Customer MVP ✅ COMPLETE + LIVE on hub.psgweb.me (promoted to main `fc6e1cc`, dpl_Wyi5; tag `psg-hub-v0.2.0`; bumped 0.2.0). v0.1 Foundation ✅ COMPLETE 2026-06-02 (tagged `v0.1.0`). Phase 3 (SendGrid + Twilio + Sanity + Vercel) shipped: transactional email + SMS with live-verified signature-checked idempotent webhooks (real `email_events` + `sms_events` rows), Sanity content backend (`vcw0bsnu`, private prod dataset), and psg-hub LIVE at https://hub.psgweb.me (branded, cert, 14 prod env keys). 03-05 closed the deferred 03-01/03-02 webhook halves + confirmed D54 decommission (data project 404; no BSM/ads-dashboard project). **One gated prod action before the Phase-3→main merge: grant Vercel GitHub-app access to the private `design-system` submodule repo (proven merge-blocker).** Phase 2 (Design system) ✅ COMPLETE + UNIFIED — psg-hub embodies the PSG design system; Phase 1 ✅ workspace consolidation.

### APPLY 10-01 execution log (for UNIFY)
- **Task 1 (auto) — DONE/PASS (AC-1):** NEW `supabase/migrations/20260608000000_google_ads_tables.sql` — 4 tables matching the blind-built read/write contracts. `google_ads_accounts` (encrypted_refresh_token bytea + key_version int + status CHECK + UNIQUE(shop_id,customer_id) = callback onConflict), `google_ads_campaigns` (account_id FK cascade, daily_budget_micros bigint, metrics jsonb, UNIQUE(shop_id,external_id)), `google_ads_oauth_states` (state_token PK + expires idx), `ads_api_call_log` (method/result CHECKs + (shop_id,method,created_at) index for the rate-limit window). RLS per-table verdict: membership SELECT `shop_id in (select public.user_shop_ids())` on accounts+campaigns (user-session reads), RLS-on/NO-policy default-deny on oauth_states+call_log (service-role only; llm_call_log/analytics_sync_runs precedent). `supabase db reset` exit 0; docker-psql verified every column/constraint/policy/index. Idempotent (drop-policy-if-exists).
- **Task 2 (auto) — DONE_WITH_CONCERNS→PASS (AC-2):** NEW `e2e/google-ads.spec.ts` schema round-trip via REAL clients against the local migrated DB (service-role writes all 4 tables + user-session RLS reads). **Concern materialized into a real finding (exactly AC-2's purpose):** the blind-built `callback/route.ts` wrote `encrypted_refresh_token: ciphertext` (raw Node Buffer); empirical probe showed PostgREST stores that as the literal `{"type":"Buffer","data":[…]}` JSON string, NOT the bytes → `decryptRefreshToken` would always fail → every linked account broken on first use. **FIX (code demonstrably wrong, migration right — deviation):** callback now writes `\\x${ciphertext.toString("hex")}` (Postgres bytea text form); `client.ts` read decodes `\\x`hex → Buffer (keeps Buffer/ArrayBuffer fallbacks). Proven: a byte-identical readback test (decode `\x`hex == original plaintext). RLS proofs: MEMBER reads 1 account + 1 campaign; NON-member reads 0/0; member reads 0 from oauth_states + call_log (default-deny). Rate-limit COUNT query runs against the real composite index. 5/5 e2e green. (Used a `\x`hex blob, not the server-only `encryptRefreshToken` import — Playwright runtime trips `import "server-only"`; crypto correctness is covered by crypto.test.ts unit. Minor deviation, documented.)
- **Task 3 (auto) — DONE/PASS (AC-3):** `dashboard/ads/page.tsx` — replaced the "coming soon" guard with the real surface: keep auth + active-shop-resolve + membership + performance-tier gate (untouched), then read `google_ads_accounts` via the user-session client (RLS) and render the built `<AccountsTable>` (empty → "No Google Ads account linked yet" + "Link Google Ads" CTA). Did NOT render `<CampaignsSection>` (it surfaces Create-campaign = mutation). E2E: OWNER shop (slug `e2e-owner-auto-body` added to `SHOP_ADS_TIER_OVERRIDE` in `.env.test.local` → performance tier) → accounts/link surface visible, coming-soon copy absent, NO Create-campaign control, axe AA clean.

## Phase 6 Plan Split (expanded 3→5 — 06-02 schema discovery 2026-06-02)

**Why 5:** 06-03 mapping found the inherited-code reconcile is far larger than a column rename — `shop_members` is phantom in ~14 files; **`google_ads_*` are phantom net-new tables** (ads = its own DDL effort); and the reviews surface assumes a schema that **diverges hard** from live (`review_items` has 0 rows + `text`/`reviewed_at`; `review_responses` lacks `tone_preset`/`version`/`safety_flags`; live `reviews` is a content-suggestion table). Operator chose full scope (gate + reviews + ads); split for reviewable/gated loops: 06-03 = spine enforcement (gate + seed), 06-04 = reviews reconcile, 06-05 = ads surface (+ google_ads_* tables).

**Grounding (read-only workflow `wf_ddd01605-c64`, 6 agents) overturned the ROADMAP premise at six points (W1–W6):** no role enum exists (free-text, zero CHECK) → DEFINE not extend; `security_profiles` is greenfield; the **BSM Phase-4 RLS base was NEVER deployed** here (psg-hub code reads phantom `shop_members`/`google_ads_*`/`agent_runs` → those customer surfaces error at runtime today); `profile_id`==`user_id`==`auth.uid()` (no conflict, W4); migrations ARE tracked remotely (5 rows) — gap is repo linkage; live admins = Nick/Tina/**Claire** (`profiles.role='admin'`), **Brian has no auth row**. The real deployed model is `shop_users(user_id, shop_id, role, location_ids[])` + helpers `user_shop_ids()`/`user_location_ids()`/`user_is_shop_owner()` (local_reach/psg-import lineage, not BSM). Customer DDL would land on a **shared prod DB holding 314,828 PII rows / 142 shops**. Full detail: `06-RESEARCH-DOSSIER.md`.

**S1/S4 gate docs (06-01 Task 3):** `06-rbac-rls-spine/PROTOCOL-migration-safety.md` (migrations-as-code is the only DDL path; read-only-MCP rule; path-A target; advisor baseline + diff gate; hard DO-NOTs) and `06-rbac-rls-spine/CHECKLIST-rls-review.md` (per-table RLS review — `to authenticated`, `(select auth.uid())`, shop/fn clamps, `private`-schema security-definer helpers, idempotency). 06-02 must follow both.

**Carry-forward gaps (found at 06-05 human-verify / close 2026-06-03):**
- **⭐ Phase 7 PREREQUISITE — onboarding bootstrap.** `shop_users` INSERT with_check = `user_is_shop_owner(shop_id)` → the first-owner row cannot be created under the browser/user-session client (chicken-and-egg on a new shop). Onboarding is the ONLY path to a `shop_users` row (06-03 also deferred its seed), so the spine is built + enforced but **un-onboardable except by manual SQL**. Phase 7's shop switcher assumes shops exist to switch between → a **service-role onboarding/bootstrap server route is a prerequisite for Phase 7, plan it first** (also reconcile onboarding's phantom shops-column INSERT: it writes website_url/phone/city/state/address which don't exist on live `shops`).
- **v0.4 billing divergence (evidence in hand).** Live `shops` has NO `stripe_customer_id` (real cols: …telephone/url/subscription_tier…). `billing/portal/route.ts` embeds `shops(stripe_customer_id)` and `webhooks/stripe/route.ts` updates `stripe_customer_id` → phantom-column, will fail when billing goes live. NOT a regression (membership repoint only; billing is v0.4 scope). Log for v0.4 so it isn't a debugging surprise.
- **Mobile nav missing (Phase 8).** Sidebar is `hidden ... lg:flex` (`src/app/dashboard/layout.tsx`) — below 1024px no nav (no hamburger/drawer), only stat cards + Sign out. Responsive app-shell gap (Phase 2 origin).
- **Dashboard HOME `agent_runs` phantom read (Phase 8).** `/dashboard` home "Agent Runs" stat card still reads phantom `agent_runs` (renders 0, swallowed — no 500). Out of 06-05 files. Same guard treatment later.
- **Test nit:** the ads-page guard has no automated test (routes mock updated, but the page guard is covered only by grep + the live check) — a future edit could silently reintroduce a phantom query. Worth a render/unit test in Phase 7/8.

**The central fork (06-01 Task 1):** the claims mechanism (D2) GATES the shared-vs-isolate call (D1). Recommended coherent path = **no-hook security-definer subquery → shared-mutate under protocol → defer the 26 anon-open policies to Phase 8**. Alternative = token-hook → isolate (separate project). A project-global token hook on the shared project is explicitly off the table (rewrites psg-advantage-portal + Claire's tokens; a throwing hook breaks login project-wide).
